				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Symphony No.7, Op.92 (Beethoven, Ludwig van)				</h1>

<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>4 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1811-1812
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Symphonies&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Symphonies</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For orchestra</a></span>; <th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>2 flutes, 2 oboes, 2 clarinets, 2 bassoons<br />2 horns, 2 trumpets, timpani, strings
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>External Links
</th>

</td></tr></table>
</div>
